import os import json import requests from datetime import datetime import time import random print("=== IMPLEMENTING RESILIENT SEARCH FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO ===") print("Phase 3: Enhanced search with rate limiting and retry logic\n") # Use existing workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace_andy_serkis_360_vr_20250806_215046' print(f"Using workspace: {workspace_dir}\n") # First, let's inspect the failed search results to understand what happened results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'andy_serkis_search_results.json') if os.path.exists(results_file): print("=== ANALYZING PREVIOUS SEARCH FAILURE ===") print(f"Results file: {os.path.basename(results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(results_file):,} bytes") # Inspect the structure first with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: previous_results = json.load(f) print("\nPrevious results structure:") for key in previous_results.keys(): if isinstance(previous_results[key], list): print(f" - {key}: {len(previous_results[key])} items") elif isinstance(previous_results[key], dict): print(f" - {key}: {len(previous_results[key])} keys") else: print(f" - {key}: {type(previous_results[key])}") # Check query results for failure patterns if 'query_results' in previous_results: failed_queries = [r for r in previous_results['query_results'] if 'http_error_429' in r.get('status', '')] print(f"\nRate limit failures: {len(failed_queries)} out of {len(previous_results['query_results'])} queries") if len(failed_queries) > 0: print("All queries failed due to rate limiting - implementing enhanced strategy") else: print("No previous results file found") # Check API key availability api_key = os.getenv('SERPAPI_API_KEY') if not api_key: print("‚ùå No SerpAPI key found") else: print("‚úÖ SerpAPI key available") # Implement enhanced search strategy with multiple approaches print("\n=== ENHANCED SEARCH STRATEGY ===") print("Approach 1: Reduced query set with extended delays") print("Approach 2: Alternative search patterns") print("Approach 3: Direct YouTube-focused searches\n") # Select the most promising queries from the original set priority_queries = [ 'Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur experience March 2018', 'site:youtube.com "Andy Serkis" 360 dinosaur 2018', '"Andy Serkis" narrator 360 degree dinosaur video 2018', 'YouTube VR dinosaurs March 2018 Serkis' ] print(f"Selected {len(priority_queries)} high-priority queries for focused search:") for i, query in enumerate(priority_queries, 1): print(f" {i}. {query}") print() # Initialize enhanced results collection enhanced_results = { 'search_metadata': { 'execution_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'search_phase': 'enhanced_with_rate_limiting', 'previous_failure': 'HTTP 429 rate limit exceeded', 'enhancement_strategy': 'reduced queries + extended delays + retry logic', 'target_criteria': { 'format': '360 VR', 'date': 'March 2018', 'content': 'Dinosaurs', 'narrator': 'Andy Serkis (Gollum voice actor)' } }, 'query_results': [], 'potential_matches': [], 'manual_search_documentation': [] } def execute_search_with_retry(query, api_key, max_retries=3): """Execute search with exponential backoff retry logic""" for attempt in range(max_retries): try: # Add random delay to avoid synchronized requests delay = (2 ** attempt) + random.uniform(1, 3) if attempt > 0: print(f" Retry attempt {attempt + 1} after {delay:.1f}s delay...") time.sleep(delay) params = { 'q': query, 'api_key': api_key, 'engine': 'google', 'google_domain': 'google.com', 'safe': 'off', 'num': 15, # Slightly fewer results to reduce load 'type': 'search' } response = requests.get('https://serpapi.com/search.json', params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: return response.json(), 'success' elif response.status_code == 429: print(f" Rate limit hit (429) - attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries}") if attempt == max_retries - 1: return None, f'rate_limit_exceeded_after_{max_retries}_attempts' continue else: return None, f'http_error_{response.status_code}' except Exception as e: print(f" Search error on attempt {attempt + 1}: {str(e)}") if attempt == max_retries - 1: return None, f'error_after_{max_retries}_attempts: {str(e)}' return None, 'max_retries_exceeded' if api_key: print("=== EXECUTING ENHANCED SEARCHES ===") for i, query in enumerate(priority_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- ENHANCED SEARCH {i}/{len(priority_queries)} ---") print(f"Query: {query}") print(f"Starting search with retry logic...") # Execute search with retry logic results, status = execute_search_with_retry(query, api_key) if status == 'success' and results: print(f"‚úÖ Search successful!") organic_results = results.get('organic_results', []) print(f"Found {len(organic_results)} organic results") # Enhanced analysis for potential matches query_matches = [] for j, result in enumerate(organic_results, 1): title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') # Enhanced criteria checking has_youtube = 'youtube.com' in link or 'youtu.be' in link has_360_vr = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ '360', 'vr', 'virtual reality', '360¬∞', '360-degree', 'immersive' ]) has_dinosaur = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'dinosaur', 'prehistoric', 'jurassic', 'cretaceous', 'triassic', 'paleontology', 'fossil', 'extinct reptile' ]) has_serkis = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'andy serkis', 'serkis', 'gollum', 'lord of the rings' ]) has_2018 = '2018' in title + ' ' + snippet has_march = 'march' in title + ' ' + snippet or 'mar 2018' in title + ' ' + snippet # Calculate enhanced match score match_score = sum([has_youtube, has_360_vr, has_dinosaur, has_serkis, has_2018, has_march]) # Lower threshold for initial detection if match_score >= 2: # At least 2 criteria match_info = { 'query_number': i, 'result_number': j, 'title': result.get('title', ''), 'snippet': result.get('snippet', ''), 'link': link, 'match_score': match_score, 'criteria_matched': { 'youtube': has_youtube, '360_vr': has_360_vr, 'dinosaur': has_dinosaur, 'andy_serkis': has_serkis, '2018': has_2018, 'march': has_march }, 'confidence_level': 'high' if match_score >= 5 else 'medium' if match_score >= 4 else 'low' } query_matches.append(match_info) print(f" üéØ MATCH {j}: {result.get('title', '')[:60]}...") print(f" Score: {match_score}/6 | Confidence: {match_info['confidence_level']}") print(f" URL: {link}") # Show which criteria matched matched_criteria = [k for k, v in match_info['criteria_matched'].items() if v] print(f" Matched: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}") if match_score >= 5: print(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH CONFIDENCE - Likely target video!") elif match_score >= 4: print(f" ‚úÖ HIGH CONFIDENCE - Strong candidate") # Store results enhanced_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'total_results': len(organic_results), 'potential_matches': len(query_matches), 'matches': query_matches, 'status': 'success' }) enhanced_results['potential_matches'].extend(query_matches) print(f"Query {i} completed: {len(query_matches)} potential matches found") else: print(f"‚ùå Search failed: {status}") enhanced_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'status': status, 'note': 'Failed despite retry logic' }) # Extended delay between queries to respect rate limits if i < len(priority_queries): delay = random.uniform(8, 12) # 8-12 second delay print(f"Waiting {delay:.1f}s before next query...") time.sleep(delay) else: print("=== DOCUMENTING MANUAL SEARCH STRATEGY ===") print("Since API is not available, documenting manual search approach:") for i, query in enumerate(priority_queries, 1): enhanced_results['manual_search_documentation'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'manual_search_instructions': f'Search Google for: {query}', 'expected_results': 'Look for YouTube videos with 360 VR, dinosaur content, Andy Serkis narration from March 2018' }) print(f"{i}. Manual search: {query}") # Analyze results print(f"\n=== ENHANCED SEARCH RESULTS ANALYSIS ===") total_matches = len(enhanced_results['potential_matches']) print(f"Total potential matches found: {total_matches}") if total_matches > 0: # Sort by match score and confidence sorted_matches = sorted( enhanced_results['potential_matches'], key=lambda x: (x['match_score'], x['confidence_level'] == 'high', x['confidence_level'] == 'medium'), reverse=True ) print(f"\nüèÜ TOP CANDIDATES FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO:") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:3], 1): # Top 3 matches print(f"\n{i}. MATCH SCORE: {match['match_score']}/6 | CONFIDENCE: {match['confidence_level'].upper()}") print(f" Title: {match['title']}") print(f" URL: {match['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {match['snippet'][:200]}...") criteria = match['criteria_matched'] matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if v] missing = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if not v] print(f" ‚úÖ Matched criteria: {', '.join(matched)}") print(f" ‚ùå Missing criteria: {', '.join(missing)}") if match['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" üéØ VERY LIKELY TARGET VIDEO - Meets most criteria!") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚≠ê STRONG CANDIDATE - High probability match") # Special analysis for YouTube links if 'youtube.com' in match['link'] or 'youtu.be' in match['link']: print(f" üì∫ CONFIRMED YOUTUBE VIDEO - Ready for verification") # Create comprehensive analysis summary enhanced_results['final_analysis'] = { 'total_queries_executed': len([r for r in enhanced_results['query_results'] if r['status'] == 'success']), 'total_potential_matches': total_matches, 'high_confidence_matches': len([m for m in enhanced_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'high']), 'medium_confidence_matches': len([m for m in enhanced_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'medium']), 'youtube_matches': len([m for m in enhanced_results['potential_matches'] if 'youtube.com' in m['link'] or 'youtu.be' in m['link']]), 'search_success': total_matches > 0 } # Save enhanced results enhanced_results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'enhanced_search_results.json') with open(enhanced_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(enhanced_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) print(f"\nüìÅ Enhanced results saved to: {os.path.basename(enhanced_results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(enhanced_results_file):,} bytes") # Create final summary with actionable results final_summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'andy_serkis_video_findings.txt') with open(final_summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write("ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO - ENHANCED SEARCH FINDINGS\n") f.write("=" * 65 + "\n\n") f.write(f"Search Date: {enhanced_results['search_metadata']['execution_date']}\n") f.write(f"Search Phase: {enhanced_results['search_metadata']['search_phase']}\n") f.write(f"Enhancement Strategy: {enhanced_results['search_metadata']['enhancement_strategy']}\n\n") f.write("TARGET CRITERIA:\n") for key, value in enhanced_results['search_metadata']['target_criteria'].items(): f.write(f" ‚úì {key.title()}: {value}\n") f.write("\n") if total_matches > 0: f.write("üéØ POTENTIAL ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEOS FOUND:\n\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:5], 1): f.write(f"{i}. {match['title']}\n") f.write(f" URL: {match['link']}\n") f.write(f" Match Score: {match['match_score']}/6\n") f.write(f" Confidence: {match['confidence_level'].title()}\n") matched_criteria = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria_matched'].items() if v] f.write(f" Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}\n") if match['match_score'] >= 5: f.write(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH PROBABILITY - Likely the target video\n") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: f.write(f" ‚úÖ HIGH PROBABILITY - Strong candidate\n") f.write("\n") f.write(f"SEARCH STATISTICS:\n") f.write(f" ‚Ä¢ Total matches found: {total_matches}\n") f.write(f" ‚Ä¢ High confidence matches: {enhanced_results['final_analysis']['high_confidence_matches']}\n") f.write(f" ‚Ä¢ YouTube video matches: {enhanced_results['final_analysis']['youtube_matches']}\n") else: f.write("‚ùå No matches found with current search strategy\n") f.write("Consider alternative approaches or manual verification\n") print(f"üìÑ Final findings saved to: {os.path.basename(final_summary_file)}") print(f"\n‚úÖ ENHANCED SEARCH COMPLETE") if total_matches > 0: high_conf = enhanced_results['final_analysis']['high_confidence_matches'] youtube_matches = enhanced_results['final_analysis']['youtube_matches'] print(f"üéâ SUCCESS: Found {total_matches} potential Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur videos") print(f"üì∫ {youtube_matches} confirmed YouTube videos for verification") if high_conf > 0: print(f"‚≠ê {high_conf} high-confidence matches likely to be the target video") print(f"üîç Review {os.path.basename(final_summary_file)} for detailed analysis and URLs") else: print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è No matches found - search strategy may need further refinement") print(f"\nüìÇ All enhanced results saved to workspace: {workspace_dir}")

have consistently failed, creating comprehensive manual search strategy\n") # Use existing workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace_andy_serkis_360_vr_20250806_215046' print(f"Using workspace: {workspace_dir}\n") # First, let's inspect the workspace to understand what we have print("=== WORKSPACE INSPECTION ===") if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f"Workspace files ({len(files)}):") for file in files: full_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(full_path): size = os.path.getsize(full_path) print(f" - {file} ({size:,} bytes)") else: print("Workspace not found, creating new one") os.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True) # Inspect the enhanced search results to understand the API failure pattern enhanced_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'enhanced_search_results.json') if os.path.exists(enhanced_file): print(f"\n=== ANALYZING ENHANCED SEARCH RESULTS ===") print(f"File: {os.path.basename(enhanced_file)}") # First inspect the structure with open(enhanced_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: enhanced_data = json.load(f) print("Enhanced results structure:") for key, value in enhanced_data.items(): if isinstance(value, dict): print(f" - {key}: dict with {len(value)} keys") elif isinstance(value, list): print(f" - {key}: list with {len(value)} items") else: print(f" - {key}: {type(value).__name__}") # Check if we have any successful results despite the failures if 'query_results' in enhanced_data: successful_queries = [q for q in enhanced_data['query_results'] if q.get('status') == 'success'] failed_queries = [q for q in enhanced_data['query_results'] if q.get('status') != 'success'] print(f"\nQuery results analysis:") print(f" - Successful queries: {len(successful_queries)}") print(f" - Failed queries: {len(failed_queries)}") if failed_queries: failure_reasons = {} for q in failed_queries: status = q.get('status', 'unknown') failure_reasons[status] = failure_reasons.get(status, 0) + 1 print(f" - Failure breakdown: {failure_reasons}") else: print("No enhanced search results file found") print("\n=== CREATING COMPREHENSIVE MANUAL SEARCH STRATEGY ===") print("Since automated API import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time from datetime import datetime import urllib.parse print("=== DIRECT WEB SCRAPING APPROACH FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO ===") print("Bypassing API limitations with direct web scraping techniques\n") # Use existing workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace_andy_serkis_360_vr_20250806_215046' print(f"Using workspace: {workspace_dir}\n") # First, inspect the workspace to understand what manual search documentation we have print("=== INSPECTING EXISTING WORKSPACE DOCUMENTATION ===") if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f"Workspace contains {len(files)} files:") for file in files: full_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(full_path): size = os.path.getsize(full_path) print(f" - {file} ({size:,} bytes)") else: print("Workspace not found, creating new one") os.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True) # Load the manual search guide to understand the search queries manual_guide_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'manual_search_guide.json') if os.path.exists(manual_guide_file): print(f"\n=== LOADING MANUAL SEARCH GUIDE ===") print(f"File: {os.path.basename(manual_guide_file)}") print(f"Size: {os.path.getsize(manual_guide_file):,} bytes") # First inspect the structure with open(manual_guide_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: manual_data = json.load(f) print("\nManual guide structure:") for key in manual_data.keys(): if isinstance(manual_data[key], dict): print(f" - {key}: dict with {len(manual_data[key])} keys") elif isinstance(manual_data[key], list): print(f" - {key}: list with {len(manual_data[key])} items") else: print(f" - {key}: {type(manual_data[key]).__name__}") # Extract search queries from the manual strategies search_queries = [] if 'manual_strategies' in manual_data: strategies = manual_data['manual_strategies'] # Extract YouTube search queries if 'direct_youtube_searches' in strategies: for search in strategies['direct_youtube_searches']: if 'search_query' in search: search_queries.append(search['search_query']) # Extract Google search queries if 'google_web_searches' in strategies: for search in strategies['google_web_searches']: if 'search_query' in search: search_queries.append(search['search_query']) print(f"\nExtracted {len(search_queries)} search queries from manual guide") for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f" {i}. {query}") else: print("Manual search guide not found, using default queries") search_queries = [ 'Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur March 2018', '"Andy Serkis" narrator dinosaur 360 2018', 'Gollum actor VR dinosaur experience' ] print(f"\n=== IMPLEMENTING DIRECT WEB SCRAPING STRATEGY ===") print("Approach: Direct Google search result scraping without API") print("Target: YouTube 360 VR videos from March 2018 with dinosaurs and Andy Serkis narration\n") # Headers to mimic a real browser headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1' } def scrape_google_search(query, max_results=20): """Scrape Google search results for a given query""" try: # Encode the query for URL encoded_query = urllib.parse.quote_plus(query) google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}' print(f" Scraping: {google_url[:100]}...") # Make request with headers response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=15) if response.status_code == 200: soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract search results results = [] # Look for search result containers (Google's HTML structure) search_containers = soup.find_all('div', class_='g') + soup.find_all('div', {'data-sokoban-container': True}) for container in search_containers: # Extract title title_elem = container.find('h3') or container.find('a') title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else '' # Extract link link_elem = container.find('a', href=True) link = link_elem['href'] if link_elem else '' # Clean up Google redirect URLs if link.startswith('/url?q='): link = urllib.parse.parse_qs(urllib.parse.urlparse(link).query).get('q', [''])[0] # Extract snippet/description snippet_elem = container.find('span') or container.find('div', class_='VwiC3b') snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else '' if title and link: results.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet }) print(f" Found {len(results)} search results") return results, 'success' else: print(f" HTTP error: {response.status_code}") return [], f'http_error_{response.status_code}' except Exception as e: print(f" Scraping error: {str(e)}") return [], f'error: {str(e)}' def analyze_result_for_criteria(result): """Analyze a search result against our target criteria""" title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') # Check criteria has_youtube = 'youtube.com' in link or 'youtu.be' in link or 'youtube' in title has_360_vr = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ '360', 'vr', 'virtual reality', '360¬∞', '360-degree', 'immersive' ]) has_dinosaur = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'dinosaur', 'prehistoric', 'jurassic', 'cretaceous', 'triassic', 'paleontology', 'fossil', 'extinct', 'reptile' ]) has_serkis = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'andy serkis', 'serkis', 'gollum', 'lord of the rings' ]) has_2018 = '2018' in title + ' ' + snippet has_march = 'march' in title + ' ' + snippet or 'mar 2018' in title + ' ' + snippet # Calculate match score match_score = sum([has_youtube, has_360_vr, has_dinosaur, has_serkis, has_2018, has_march]) return { 'match_score': match_score, 'criteria_matched': { 'youtube': has_youtube, '360_vr': has_360_vr, 'dinosaur': has_dinosaur, 'andy_serkis': has_serkis, '2018': has_2018, 'march': has_march }, 'confidence_level': 'high' if match_score >= 5 else 'medium' if match_score >= 4 else 'low' if match_score >= 2 else 'none' } # Initialize results collection scraping_results = { 'search_metadata': { 'execution_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'method': 'direct_web_scraping', 'target_criteria': { 'format': '360 VR', 'date': 'March 2018', 'content': 'Dinosaurs', 'narrator': 'Andy Serkis (Gollum voice actor)' }, 'total_queries': len(search_queries) }, 'query_results': [], 'potential_matches': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } print("=== EXECUTING WEB SCRAPING SEARCHES ===") for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- SCRAPING SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)} ---") print(f"Query: {query}") # Execute scraping results, status = scrape_google_search(query) if status == 'success' and results: print(f"‚úÖ Scraping successful - {len(results)} results found") # Analyze results for potential matches query_matches = [] for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): analysis = analyze_result_for_criteria(result) # Only consider results with some match potential if analysis['match_score'] >= 2: match_info = { 'query_number': i, 'result_number': j, 'title': result['title'], 'snippet': result['snippet'], 'link': result['link'], **analysis } query_matches.append(match_info) print(f" üéØ POTENTIAL MATCH {j}: {result['title'][:60]}...") print(f" Score: {analysis['match_score']}/6 | Confidence: {analysis['confidence_level']}") print(f" URL: {result['link']}") # Show matched criteria matched_criteria = [k for k, v in analysis['criteria_matched'].items() if v] print(f" Matched: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}") if analysis['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH CONFIDENCE - Likely target video!") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚úÖ HIGH CONFIDENCE - Strong candidate") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 3: print(f" ‚ö†Ô∏è MEDIUM CONFIDENCE - Possible match") # Store results scraping_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'total_results': len(results), 'potential_matches': len(query_matches), 'matches': query_matches, 'status': 'success' }) scraping_results['potential_matches'].extend(query_matches) print(f"Query {i} completed: {len(query_matches)} potential matches found") else: print(f"‚ùå Scraping failed: {status}") scraping_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'status': status, 'note': 'Web scraping failed' }) # Respectful delay between requests if i < len(search_queries): delay = 3 # 3 second delay print(f"Waiting {delay}s before next query...") time.sleep(delay) # Analyze and summarize results print(f"\n=== WEB SCRAPING RESULTS ANALYSIS ===") total_matches = len(scraping_results['potential_matches']) print(f"Total potential matches found: {total_matches}") if total_matches > 0: # Sort by match score and confidence sorted_matches = sorted( scraping_results['potential_matches'], key=lambda x: (x['match_score'], x['confidence_level'] == 'high'), reverse=True ) print(f"\nüèÜ TOP CANDIDATES FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO:") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:5], 1): # Top 5 matches print(f"\n{i}. MATCH SCORE: {match['match_score']}/6 | CONFIDENCE: {match['confidence_level'].upper()}") print(f" Title: {match['title']}") print(f" URL: {match['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {match['snippet'][:200]}...") criteria = match['criteria_matched'] matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if v] missing = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if not v] print(f" ‚úÖ Matched: {', '.join(matched)}") print(f" ‚ùå Missing: {', '.join(missing)}") # Special handling for YouTube links if 'youtube.com' in match['link'] or 'youtu.be' in match['link']: print(f" üì∫ CONFIRMED YOUTUBE VIDEO - Ready for verification") # Extract video ID if possible if 'watch?v=' in match['link']: video_id = match['link'].split('watch?v=')[1].split('&')[0] print(f" üÜî Video ID: {video_id}") if match['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" üéØ VERY LIKELY TARGET VIDEO!") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚≠ê STRONG CANDIDATE") # Create analysis summary scraping_results['analysis_summary'] = { 'total_queries_executed': len([r for r in scraping_results['query_results'] if r['status'] == 'success']), 'total_potential_matches': total_matches, 'high_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'high']), 'medium_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'medium']), 'youtube_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if 'youtube.com' in m['link'] or 'youtu.be' in m['link']]), 'search_success': total_matches > 0 } # Save comprehensive scraping results scraping_results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'web_scraping_results.json') with open(scraping_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(scraping_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) print(f"\nüìÅ Web scraping results saved to: {os.path.basename(scraping_results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(scraping_results_file):,} bytes") # Create final findings summary if total_matches > 0: findings_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'ANDY_SERKIS_VIDEO_FINDINGS.txt') with open(findings_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write("ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO - WEB SCRAPING FINDINGS\n") f.write("=" * 60 + "\n\n") f.write(f"Search Date: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['execution_date']}\n") f.write(f"Method: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['method']}\n") f.write(f"Total Matches Found: {total_matches}\n\n") f.write("üéØ TARGET CRITERIA:\n") for key, value in scraping_results['search_metadata']['target_criteria'].items(): f.write(f" ‚úì {key.title()}: {value}\n") f.write("\n") f.write("üèÜ TOP CANDIDATE VIDEOS:\n\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:3], 1): f.write(f"{i}. {match['title']}\n") f.write(f" URL: {match['link']}\n") f.write(f" Match Score: {match['match_score']}/6\n") f.write(f" Confidence: {match['confidence_level'].title()}\n") matched_criteria = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria_matched'].items() if v] f.write(f" Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}\n") if match['match_score'] >= 5: f.write(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH PROBABILITY - Likely the target video\n") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: f.write(f" ‚úÖ HIGH PROBABILITY - Strong candidate\n") f.write("\n") f.write(f"SEARCH STATISTICS:\n") f.write(f" ‚Ä¢ Total matches: {total_matches}\n") f.write(f" ‚Ä¢ High confidence: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['high_confidence_matches']}\n") f.write(f" ‚Ä¢ YouTube videos: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['youtube_matches']}\n") print(f"üìÑ Final findings saved to: {os.path.basename(findings_file)}") print(f"\n‚úÖ WEB SCRAPING SEARCH COMPLETE") if total_matches > 0: high_conf = scraping_results['analysis_summary']['high_confidence_matches'] youtube_matches = scraping_results['analysis_summary']['youtube_matches'] print(f"üéâ SUCCESS: Found {total_matches} potential Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur videos") print(f"üì∫ {youtube_matches} confirmed YouTube videos identified") if high_conf > 0: print(f"‚≠ê {high_conf} high-confidence matches found") print(f"\nüîç NEXT STEPS: Verify the top candidates by:") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Visiting the YouTube URLs") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Confirming 360 VR format (look for 360¬∞ controls)") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Checking publication date is March 2018") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Listening for Andy Serkis narration") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Verifying dinosaur content") else: print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è No matches found with web scraping approach") print(f"Consider refining search terms or trying alternative methods") print(f"\nüìÇ All web scraping results saved to workspace: {workspace_dir}")

Extract title title_elem = container.find('h3') or container.find('a') title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else '' # Extract link link_elem = container.find('a', href=True) link = link_elem['href'] if link_elem else '' # Clean up Google redirect URLs if link.startswith('/url?q='): link = urllib.parse.parse_qs(urllib.parse.urlparse(link).query).get('q', [''])[0] # Extract snippet/description snippet_elem = container.find('span') or container.find('div', class_='VwiC3b') snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else '' if title and link: results.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet }) print(f" Found {len(results)} search results") return results, 'success' else: print(f" HTTP error: {response.status_code}") return [], f'http_error_{response.status_code}' except Exception as e: print(f" Scraping error: {str(e)}") return [], f'error: {str(e)}' def analyze_result_for_criteria(result): """Analyze a search result against our target criteria""" title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') # Check criteria has_youtube = 'youtube.com' in link or 'youtu.be' in link or 'youtube' in title has_360_vr = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ '360', 'vr', 'virtual reality', '360¬∞', '360-degree', 'immersive' ]) has_dinosaur = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'dinosaur', 'prehistoric', 'jurassic', 'cretaceous', 'triassic', 'paleontology', 'fossil', 'extinct', 'reptile' ]) has_serkis = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'andy serkis', 'serkis', 'gollum', 'lord of the rings' ]) has_2018 = '2018' in title + ' ' + snippet has_march = 'march' in title + ' ' + snippet or 'mar 2018' in title + ' ' + snippet # Calculate match score match_score = sum([has_youtube, has_360_vr, has_dinosaur, has_serkis, has_2018, has_march]) return { 'match_score': match_score, 'criteria_matched': { 'youtube': has_youtube, '360_vr': has_360_vr, 'dinosaur': has_dinosaur, 'andy_serkis': has_serkis, '2018': has_2018, 'march': has_march }, 'confidence_level': 'high' if match_score >= 5 else 'medium' if match_score >= 4 else 'low' if match_score >= 2 else 'none' } # Initialize results collection scraping_results = { 'search_metadata': { 'execution_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'method': 'direct_web_scraping', 'target_criteria': { 'format': '360 VR', 'date': 'March 2018', 'content': 'Dinosaurs', 'narrator': 'Andy Serkis (Gollum voice actor)' }, 'total_queries': len(search_queries) }, 'query_results': [], 'potential_matches': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } print("=== EXECUTING WEB SCRAPING SEARCHES ===") for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- SCRAPING SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)} ---") print(f"Query: {query}") # Execute scraping results, status = scrape_google_search(query) if status == 'success' and results: print(f"‚úÖ Scraping successful - {len(results)} results found") # Analyze results for potential matches query_matches = [] for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): analysis = analyze_result_for_criteria(result) # Only consider results with some match potential if analysis['match_score'] >= 2: match_info = { 'query_number': i, 'result_number': j, 'title': result['title'], 'snippet': result['snippet'], 'link': result['link'], **analysis } query_matches.append(match_info) print(f" üéØ POTENTIAL MATCH {j}: {result['title'][:60]}...") print(f" Score: {analysis['match_score']}/6 | Confidence: {analysis['confidence_level']}") print(f" URL: {result['link']}") # Show matched criteria matched_criteria = [k for k, v in analysis['criteria_matched'].items() if v] print(f" Matched: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}") if analysis['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH CONFIDENCE - Likely target video!") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚úÖ HIGH CONFIDENCE - Strong candidate") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 3: print(f" ‚ö†Ô∏è MEDIUM CONFIDENCE - Possible match") # Store results scraping_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'total_results': len(results), 'potential_matches': len(query_matches), 'matches': query_matches, 'status': 'success' }) scraping_results['potential_matches'].extend(query_matches) print(f"Query {i} completed: {len(query_matches)} potential matches found") else: print(f"‚ùå Scraping failed: {status}") scraping_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'status': status, 'note': 'Web scraping failed' }) # Respectful delay between requests if i < len(search_queries): delay = 3 # 3 second delay print(f"Waiting {delay}s before next query...") time.sleep(delay) # Analyze and summarize results print(f"\n=== WEB SCRAPING RESULTS ANALYSIS ===") total_matches = len(scraping_results['potential_matches']) print(f"Total potential matches found: {total_matches}") if total_matches > 0: # Sort by match score and confidence sorted_matches = sorted( scraping_results['potential_matches'], key=lambda x: (x['match_score'], x['confidence_level'] == 'high'), reverse=True ) print(f"\nüèÜ TOP CANDIDATES FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO:") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:5], 1): # Top 5 matches print(f"\n{i}. MATCH SCORE: {match['match_score']}/6 | CONFIDENCE: {match['confidence_level'].upper()}") print(f" Title: {match['title']}") print(f" URL: {match['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {match['snippet'][:200]}...") criteria = match['criteria_matched'] matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if v] missing = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if not v] print(f" ‚úÖ Matched: {', '.join(matched)}") print(f" ‚ùå Missing: {', '.join(missing)}") # Special handling for YouTube links if 'youtube.com' in match['link'] or 'youtu.be' in match['link']: print(f" üì∫ CONFIRMED YOUTUBE VIDEO - Ready for verification") # Extract video ID if possible if 'watch?v=' in match['link']: video_id = match['link'].split('watch?v=')[1].split('&')[0] print(f" üÜî Video ID: {video_id}") if match['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" üéØ VERY LIKELY TARGET VIDEO!") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚≠ê STRONG CANDIDATE") # Create analysis summary scraping_results['analysis_summary'] = { 'total_queries_executed': len([r for r in scraping_results['query_results'] if r['status'] == 'success']), 'total_potential_matches': total_matches, 'high_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'high']), 'medium_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'medium']), 'youtube_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if 'youtube.com' in m['link'] or 'youtu.be' in m['link']]), 'search_success': total_matches > 0 } # Save comprehensive scraping results scraping_results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'web_scraping_results.json') with open(scraping_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(scraping_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) print(f"\nüìÅ Web scraping results saved to: {os.path.basename(scraping_results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(scraping_results_file):,} bytes") # Create final findings summary if total_matches > 0: findings_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'ANDY_SERKIS_VIDEO_FINDINGS.txt') with open(findings_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write("ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO - WEB SCRAPING FINDINGS\n") f.write("=" * 60 + "\n\n") f.write(f"Search Date: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['execution_date']}\n") f.write(f"Method: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['method']}\n") f.write(f"Total Matches Found: {total_matches}\n\n") f.write("üéØ TARGET CRITERIA:\n") for key, value in scraping_results['search_metadata']['target_criteria'].items(): f.write(f" ‚úì {key.title()}: {value}\n") f.write("\n") f.write("üèÜ TOP CANDIDATE VIDEOS:\n\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:3], 1): f.write(f"{i}. {match['title']}\n") f.write(f" URL: {match['link']}\n") f.write(f" Match Score: {match['match_score']}/6\n") f.write(f" Confidence: {match['confidence_level'].title()}\n") matched_criteria = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria_matched'].items() if v] f.write(f" Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}\n") if match['match_score'] >= 5: f.write(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH PROBABILITY - import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time from datetime import datetime import urllib.parse print("=== FIXED WEB SCRAPING APPROACH FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO ===") print("Correcting variable scope issue and implementing working web scraper\n") # Use existing workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace_andy_serkis_360_vr_20250806_215046' print(f"Using workspace: {workspace_dir}\n") # Define headers BEFORE the function that uses them (fixing the scope error) headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1' } print("‚úÖ Browser headers configured for web scraping") # Encode the query for URL encoded_query = urllib.parse.quote_plus(query) google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}' print(f" Requesting: {google_url[:80]}...") # Make request with headers (now properly defined above) response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úÖ HTTP 200 - Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes") soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract search results using multiple selectors results = [] # Try different Google result selectors search_selectors = [ 'div.g', # Standard Google result container 'div[data-sokoban-container]', # Alternative container 'div.tF2Cxc', # Another common selector 'div.yuRUbf' # Link container ] search_containers = [] for selector in search_selectors: containers = soup.select(selector) if containers: search_containers.extend(containers) print(f" Found {len(containers)} results with selector: {selector}") # Remove duplicates while preserving order seen = set() unique_containers = [] for container in search_containers: container_text = container.get_text()[:100] # Use first 100 chars as identifier if container_text not in seen: seen.add(container_text) unique_containers.append(container) print(f" Processing {len(unique_containers)} unique result containers") for i, container in enumerate(unique_containers[:max_results], 1): # Extract title - try multiple approaches title = '' title_selectors = ['h3', 'a h3', 'div h3', '[role="heading"]'] for selector in title_selectors: title_elem = container.select_one(selector) if title_elem: title = title_elem.get_text().strip() break # Extract link - try multiple approaches link = '' link_elem = container.find('a', href=True) if link_elem: link = link_elem.get('href', '') # Clean up Google redirect URLs if link.startswith('/url?q='): try: parsed = urllib.parse.parse_qs(urllib.parse.urlparse(link).query) link = parsed.get('q', [''])[0] except: pass # Keep original link if parsing fails # Extract snippet/description snippet = '' snippet_selectors = ['.VwiC3b', '.s3v9rd', '.st', 'span'] for selector in snippet_selectors: snippet_elem = container.select_one(selector) if snippet_elem: snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if len(snippet) > 20: # Only use substantial snippets break if title and link and not link.startswith('#'): results.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'result_number': i }) print(f" [{i}] {title[:50]}... | {link[:60]}...") print(f" ‚úÖ Extracted {len(results)} valid search results") return results, 'success' else: print(f" ‚ùå HTTP error: {response.status_code}") return [], f'http_error_{response.status_code}' except Exception as e: print(f" ‚ùå Scraping error: {str(e)}") return [], f'error: {str(e)}' def analyze_result_for_criteria(result): """Analyze a search result against our target criteria""" title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') # import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time from datetime import datetime import urllib.parse print("=== FIXED WEB SCRAPING APPROACH FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO ===") print("Correcting variable scope issue and implementing working web scraper\n") # Use existing workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace_andy_serkis_360_vr_20250806_215046' print(f"Using workspace: {workspace_dir}\n") # Define headers BEFORE the function that uses them (fixing the scope error) headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1' } print("‚úÖ Browser headers configured for web scraping") # First, inspect the manual search guide to extract queries manual_guide_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'manual_search_guide.json') if os.path.exists(manual_guide_file): print(f"\n=== LOADING SEARCH QUERIES FROM MANUAL GUIDE ===") print(f"File: {os.path.basename(manual_guide_file)}") print(f"Size: {os.path.getsize(manual_guide_file):,} bytes") # First inspect the structure with open(manual_guide_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: content = f.read() print(f"Content length: {len(content)} characters") # Parse JSON manual_data = json.loads(content) print("\nManual guide keys:") for key in manual_data.keys(): if isinstance(manual_data[key], dict): print(f" - {key}: dict with {len(manual_data[key])} keys") elif isinstance(manual_data[key], list): print(f" - {key}: list with {len(manual_data[key])} items") else: print(f" - {key}: {type(manual_data[key]).__name__}") # Extract search queries from manual strategies search_queries = [] if 'manual_strategies' in manual_data: strategies = manual_data['manual_strategies'] print(f"\nFound manual_strategies with {len(strategies)} strategy types") # Extract from direct YouTube searches if 'direct_youtube_searches' in strategies: youtube_searches = strategies['direct_youtube_searches'] print(f"Found {len(youtube_searches)} YouTube search strategies") for search in youtube_searches: if 'search_query' in search: search_queries.append(search['search_query']) print(f" + {search['search_query']}") # Extract from Google web searches if 'google_web_searches' in strategies: google_searches = strategies['google_web_searches'] print(f"Found {len(google_searches)} Google search strategies") for search in google_searches: if 'search_query' in search: search_queries.append(search['search_query']) print(f" + {search['search_query']}") print(f"\nTotal extracted queries: {len(search_queries)}") else: print("Manual search guide not found, using default queries") search_queries = [ 'Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur March 2018', '"Andy Serkis" narrator dinosaur 360 2018', 'Gollum actor VR dinosaur experience' ] def scrape_google_search(query, max_results=15): """Scrape Google search results for a given query""" try: # Encode the query for URL encoded_query = urllib.parse.quote_plus(query) google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}' print(f" Requesting: {google_url[:80]}...") # Make request with headers (now properly defined above) response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úÖ HTTP 200 - Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes") soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract search results using multiple selectors results = [] # Try different Google result selectors search_selectors = [ 'div.g', # Standard Google result container 'div[data-sokoban-container]', # Alternative container 'div.tF2Cxc', # Another common selector 'div.yuRUbf' # Link container ] search_containers = [] for selector in search_selectors: containers = soup.select(selector) if containers: search_containers.extend(containers) print(f" Found {len(containers)} results with selector: {selector}") # Remove duplicates while preserving order seen = set() unique_containers = [] for container in search_containers: container_text = container.get_text()[:100] # Use first 100 chars as identifier if container_text not in seen: seen.add(container_text) unique_containers.append(container) print(f" Processing {len(unique_containers)} unique result containers") for i, container in enumerate(unique_containers[:max_results], 1): # Extract title - try multiple approaches title = '' title_selectors = ['h3', 'a h3', 'div h3', '[role="heading"]'] for selector in title_selectors: title_elem = container.select_one(selector) if title_elem: title = title_elem.get_text().strip() break # Extract link - try multiple approaches link = '' link_elem = container.find('a', href=True) if link_elem: link = link_elem.get('href', '') # Clean up Google redirect URLs if link.startswith('/url?q='): try: parsed = urllib.parse.parse_qs(urllib.parse.urlparse(link).query) link = parsed.get('q', [''])[0] except: pass # Keep original link if parsing fails # Extract snippet/description snippet = '' snippet_selectors = ['.VwiC3b', '.s3v9rd', '.st', 'span'] for selector in snippet_selectors: snippet_elem = container.select_one(selector) if snippet_elem: snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if len(snippet) > 20: # Only use substantial snippets break if title and link and not link.startswith('#'): results.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'result_number': i }) print(f" [{i}] {title[:50]}... | {link[:60]}...") print(f" ‚úÖ Extracted {len(results)} valid search results") return results, 'success' else: print(f" ‚ùå HTTP error: {response.status_code}") return [], f'http_error_{response.status_code}' except Exception as e: print(f" ‚ùå Scraping error: {str(e)}") return [], f'error: {str(e)}' def analyze_result_for_criteria(result): """Analyze a search result against our target criteria""" title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') # Enhanced criteria checking has_youtube = ('youtube.com' in link or 'youtu.be' in link or 'youtube' in title or 'youtube' in snippet) has_360_vr = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ '360', 'vr', 'virtual reality', '360¬∞', '360-degree', 'immersive', 'virtual', '360 video', 'vr video' ]) has_dinosaur = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'dinosaur', 'prehistoric', 'jurassic', 'cretaceous', 'triassic', 'paleontology', 'fossil', 'extinct', 'reptile', 'mesozoic' ]) has_serkis = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'andy serkis', 'serkis', 'gollum', 'lord of the rings', 'andy', 'narrator' ]) has_2018 = '2018' in title + ' ' + snippet or '2018' in link has_march = ('march' in title + ' ' + snippet or 'mar 2018' in title + ' ' + snippet or 'march 2018' in title + ' ' + snippet) # Calculate match score match_score = sum([has_youtube, has_360_vr, has_dinosaur, has_serkis, has_2018, has_march]) return { 'match_score': match_score, 'criteria_matched': { 'youtube': has_youtube, '360_vr': has_360_vr, 'dinosaur': has_dinosaur, 'andy_serkis': has_serkis, '2018': has_2018, 'march': has_march }, 'confidence_level': ( 'very_high' if match_score >= 5 else 'high' if match_score >= 4 else 'medium' if match_score >= 3 else 'low' if match_score >= 2 else 'none' ) } # Initialize results collection scraping_results = { 'search_metadata': { 'execution_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'method': 'fixed_web_scraping', 'fix_applied': 'Corrected headers variable scope issue', 'target_criteria': { 'format': '360 VR', 'date': 'March 2018', 'content': 'Dinosaurs', 'narrator': 'Andy Serkis (Gollum voice actor)' }, 'total_queries': len(search_queries) }, 'query_results': [], 'potential_matches': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } print(f"\n=== EXECUTING FIXED WEB SCRAPING SEARCHES ===") print(f"Target: YouTube 360 VR videos from March 2018 with dinosaurs and Andy Serkis narration") print(f"Queries to execute: {len(search_queries)}\n") for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- SCRAPING SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)} ---") print(f"Query: '{query}'") # Execute scraping with fixed headers results, status = scrape_google_search(query) if status == 'success' and results: print(f"‚úÖ Scraping successful - {len(results)} results obtained") # Analyze results for potential matches query_matches = [] for result in results: analysis = analyze_result_for_criteria(result) # Consider results with at least 2 criteria matches if analysis['match_score'] >= 2: match_info = { 'query_number': i, 'result_number': result.get('result_number', 0), 'title': result['title'], 'snippet': result['snippet'], 'link': result['link'], **analysis } query_matches.append(match_info) print(f" üéØ MATCH #{result.get('result_number', '?')}: {result['title'][:60]}...") print(f" Score: {analysis['match_score']}/6 | Confidence: {analysis['confidence_level']}") print(f" URL: {result['link'][:80]}...") # Show matched criteria matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in analysis['criteria_matched'].items() if v] missing = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in analysis['criteria_matched'].items() if not v] print(f" ‚úÖ Matched: {', '.join(matched)}") print(f" ‚ùå Missing: {', '.join(missing)}") if analysis['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH CONFIDENCE - Likely target video!") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚úÖ HIGH CONFIDENCE - Strong candidate") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 3: print(f" ‚ö†Ô∏è MEDIUM CONFIDENCE - Possible match") # Special handling for YouTube links if 'youtube.com' in result['link'] or 'youtu.be' in result['link']: print(f" üì∫ CONFIRMED YOUTUBE VIDEO") # Try to extract video ID if 'watch?v=' in result['link']: try: video_id = result['link'].split('watch?v=')[1].split('&')[0] print(f" üÜî Video ID: {video_id}") except: pass print() # Add spacing # Store results scraping_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'total_results': len(results), 'potential_matches': len(query_matches), 'matches': query_matches, 'status': 'success' }) scraping_results['potential_matches'].extend(query_matches) print(f"Query {i} completed: {len(query_matches)} potential matches found") else: print(f"‚ùå Scraping failed: {status}") scraping_results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'status': status, 'note': 'Web scraping failed' }) # Respectful delay between requests if i < len(search_queries): delay = 4 # 4 second delay to be respectful print(f"Waiting {delay}s before next query...") time.sleep(delay) # Analyze and summarize results print(f"\n=== COMPREHENSIVE RESULTS ANALYSIS ===") total_matches = len(scraping_results['potential_matches']) print(f"Total potential matches found: {total_matches}") if total_matches > 0: # Sort by match score and confidence sorted_matches = sorted( scraping_results['potential_matches'], key=lambda x: (x['match_score'], x['confidence_level'] == 'very_high', x['confidence_level'] == 'high'), reverse=True ) print(f"\nüèÜ TOP CANDIDATES FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO:") print(f"(Sorted by match score and confidence level)\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:5], 1): # Show top 5 matches print(f"{i}. MATCH SCORE: {match['match_score']}/6 | CONFIDENCE: {match['confidence_level'].upper().replace('_', ' ')}") print(f" Title: {match['title']}") print(f" URL: {match['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {match['snippet'][:200]}..." if match['snippet'] else " Snippet: (no description available)") criteria = match['criteria_matched'] matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if v] missing = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in criteria.items() if not v] print(f" ‚úÖ Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched)}") print(f" ‚ùå Missing: {', '.join(missing)}") # Special handling for YouTube links if 'youtube.com' in match['link'] or 'youtu.be' in match['link']: print(f" üì∫ CONFIRMED YOUTUBE VIDEO - Ready for verification") # Extract video ID if possible if 'watch?v=' in match['link']: try: video_id = match['link'].split('watch?v=')[1].split('&')[0] print(f" üÜî Video ID: {video_id}") print(f" üîó Direct link: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}") except: pass if match['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" üéØ VERY LIKELY TARGET VIDEO - Meets most criteria!") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚≠ê STRONG CANDIDATE - High probability match") elif match['match_score'] >= 3: print(f" ‚úÖ GOOD CANDIDATE - Worth investigating") print() # Add spacing between matches # Create analysis summary scraping_results['analysis_summary'] = { 'total_queries_executed': len([r for r in scraping_results['query_results'] if r['status'] == 'success']), 'total_potential_matches': total_matches, 'very_high_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'very_high']), 'high_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'high']), 'medium_confidence_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if m['confidence_level'] == 'medium']), 'youtube_matches': len([m for m in scraping_results['potential_matches'] if 'youtube.com' in m['link'] or 'youtu.be' in m['link']]), 'search_success': total_matches > 0, 'top_match_score': sorted_matches[0]['match_score'] if sorted_matches else 0, 'top_match_confidence': sorted_matches[0]['confidence_level'] if sorted_matches else 'none' } print(f"üìä SEARCH STATISTICS:") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Total matches: {total_matches}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Very high confidence: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['very_high_confidence_matches']}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ High confidence: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['high_confidence_matches']}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Medium confidence: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['medium_confidence_matches']}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ YouTube videos: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['youtube_matches']}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Top match score: {scraping_results['analysis_summary']['top_match_score']}/6") else: scraping_results['analysis_summary'] = { 'total_queries_executed': len([r for r in scraping_results['query_results'] if r['status'] == 'success']), 'total_potential_matches': 0, 'search_success': False } print(f"‚ùå No potential matches found") # Save comprehensive scraping results scraping_results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'fixed_web_scraping_results.json') with open(scraping_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(scraping_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) print(f"\nüìÅ Scraping results saved to: {os.path.basename(scraping_results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(scraping_results_file):,} bytes") # Create actionable findings report if total_matches > 0: findings_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'ANDY_SERKIS_VIDEO_CANDIDATES.txt') with open(findings_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write("ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO - CANDIDATE FINDINGS\n") f.write("=" * 65 + "\n\n") f.write(f"Search Date: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['execution_date']}\n") f.write(f"Method: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['method']}\n") f.write(f"Fix Applied: {scraping_results['search_metadata']['fix_applied']}\n") f.write(f"Total Candidates Found: {total_matches}\n\n") f.write("üéØ TARGET CRITERIA:\n") for key, value in scraping_results['search_metadata']['target_criteria'].items(): f.write(f" ‚úì {key.title()}: {value}\n") f.write("\n") f.write("üèÜ TOP CANDIDATE VIDEOS FOR VERIFICATION:\n\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:5], 1): f.write(f"{i}. {match['title']}\n") f.write(f" URL: {match['link']}\n") f.write(f" Match Score: {match['match_score']}/6\n") f.write(f" Confidence: {match['confidence_level'].replace('_', ' ').title()}\n") matched_criteria = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria_matched'].items() if v] f.write(f" Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched_criteria)}\n") if match['match_score'] >= 5: f.write(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH PROBABILITY - Likely the target video\n") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: f.write(f" ‚úÖ HIGH PROBABILITY - Strong candidate\n") elif match['match_score'] >= 3: f.write(f" ‚ö†Ô∏è MEDIUM PROBABILITY - Worth checking\n") f.write(f"\n VERIFICATION STEPS:\n") f.write(f" 1. import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time from datetime import datetime import urllib.parse print("=== PROPERLY FIXED WEB SCRAPING FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO ===") print("Correcting the persistent variable scope issue and implementing working scraper\n") # Use existing workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace_andy_serkis_360_vr_20250806_215046' print(f"Using workspace: {workspace_dir}\n") # CRITICAL FIX: Define headers at the TOP of the script, before any functions headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } print("‚úÖ Headers properly defined at script top (fixing scope issue)") # First, inspect the manual search guide structure before loading manual_guide_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'manual_search_guide.json') if os.path.exists(manual_guide_file): print(f"\n=== INSPECTING MANUAL SEARCH GUIDE STRUCTURE ===") print(f"File: {os.path.basename(manual_guide_file)}") print(f"Size: {os.path.getsize(manual_guide_file):,} bytes") # First read and inspect the JSON structure with open(manual_guide_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: content = f.read() print(f"Content preview: {content[:200]}...") # Parse and inspect structure try: manual_data = json.loads(content) print(f"\nJSON structure successfully parsed:") for key, value in manual_data.items(): if isinstance(value, dict): print(f" - {key}: dict with keys {list(value.keys())[:3]}...") elif isinstance(value, list): print(f" - {key}: list with {len(value)} items") else: print(f" - {key}: {type(value).__name__} = {str(value)[:50]}...") # Extract search queries carefully search_queries = [] if 'manual_strategies' in manual_data: strategies = manual_data['manual_strategies'] print(f"\nExtracting queries from manual_strategies:") # Extract from direct YouTube searches if 'direct_youtube_searches' in strategies: youtube_searches = strategies['direct_youtube_searches'] print(f"Found {len(youtube_searches)} YouTube search strategies") for i, search in enumerate(youtube_searches): if isinstance(search, dict) and 'search_query' in search: query = search['search_query'] search_queries.append(query) print(f" {len(search_queries)}. {query}") # Extract from Google web searches if 'google_web_searches' in strategies: google_searches = strategies['google_web_searches'] print(f"Found {len(google_searches)} Google search strategies") for i, search in enumerate(google_searches): if isinstance(search, dict) and 'search_query' in search: query = search['search_query'] search_queries.append(query) print(f" {len(search_queries)}. {query}") print(f"\nTotal queries extracted: {len(search_queries)}") except json.JSONDecodeError as e: print(f"‚ùå JSON parsing error: {e}") search_queries = [] else: print("Manual search guide not found, using fallback queries") search_queries = [] # Fallback queries if extraction failed if not search_queries: print("\nUsing fallback search queries:") search_queries = [ 'Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur March 2018', '"Andy Serkis" narrator dinosaur 360 2018', 'Gollum actor VR dinosaur experience', 'site:youtube.com "Andy Serkis" 360 dinosaur 2018' ] for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f" {i}. {query}") def scrape_google_search(query, max_results=10): """Scrape Google search results - headers now properly accessible""" try: # Encode query for URL encoded_query = urllib.parse.quote_plus(query) google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}' print(f" Requesting: {google_url[:70]}...") # Make request - headers variable is now properly defined above response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=15) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úÖ Success - Content: {len(response.content):,} bytes") soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') results = [] # Use multiple selectors to find search results result_containers = ( soup.select('div.g') + # Standard results soup.select('div.tF2Cxc') + # Alternative layout soup.select('div[data-sokoban-container]') # Another layout ) print(f" Found {len(result_containers)} result containers") for i, container in enumerate(result_containers[:max_results], 1): # Extract title title_elem = container.select_one('h3') or container.select_one('a') title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else '' # Extract link link_elem = container.select_one('a[href]') link = '' if link_elem: link = link_elem.get('href', '') # Clean Google redirect URLs if link.startswith('/url?q='): try: parsed = urllib.parse.parse_qs(urllib.parse.urlparse(link).query) link = parsed.get('q', [''])[0] except: pass # Extract snippet snippet_elem = ( container.select_one('.VwiC3b') or container.select_one('.s3v9rd') or container.select_one('span') ) snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else '' if title and link and not link.startswith('#'): results.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'position': i }) print(f" [{i}] {title[:40]}... | {link[:50]}...") print(f" ‚úÖ Extracted {len(results)} valid results") return results, 'success' else: print(f" ‚ùå HTTP {response.status_code}") return [], f'http_{response.status_code}' except Exception as e: print(f" ‚ùå Error: {str(e)}") return [], f'error: {str(e)}' def analyze_result(result): """Analyze search result against Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur criteria""" title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') # Check each criterion has_youtube = 'youtube.com' in link or 'youtu.be' in link or 'youtube' in title has_360_vr = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ '360', 'vr', 'virtual reality', '360¬∞', '360-degree', 'immersive' ]) has_dinosaur = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'dinosaur', 'prehistoric', 'jurassic', 'cretaceous', 'fossil', 'extinct' ]) has_serkis = any(term in title + ' ' + snippet for term in [ 'andy serkis', 'serkis', 'gollum', 'narrator' ]) has_2018 = '2018' in title + ' ' + snippet or '2018' in link has_march = 'march' in title + ' ' + snippet or 'mar 2018' in title + ' ' + snippet # Calculate match score criteria = { 'youtube': has_youtube, '360_vr': has_360_vr, 'dinosaur': has_dinosaur, 'andy_serkis': has_serkis, '2018': has_2018, 'march': has_march } match_score = sum(criteria.values()) confidence = ( 'very_high' if match_score >= 5 else 'high' if match_score >= 4 else 'medium' if match_score >= 3 else 'low' if match_score >= 2 else 'none' ) return { 'match_score': match_score, 'criteria': criteria, 'confidence': confidence } # Initialize results results = { 'search_metadata': { 'execution_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'method': 'corrected_web_scraping', 'fix_applied': 'Headers defined before function definitions', 'target': 'YouTube 360 VR dinosaur video from March 2018 with Andy Serkis narration', 'queries_count': len(search_queries) }, 'query_results': [], 'all_matches': [], 'summary': {} } print(f"\n=== EXECUTING CORRECTED WEB SCRAPING ===") print(f"Target: YouTube 360 VR dinosaur video from March 2018 with Andy Serkis narration") print(f"Queries to process: {len(search_queries)}\n") for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)} ---") print(f"Query: '{query}'") # Execute search with properly scoped headers search_results, status = scrape_google_search(query) if status == 'success' and search_results: print(f"‚úÖ Search successful - {len(search_results)} results") # Analyze each result query_matches = [] for result in search_results: analysis = analyze_result(result) # Only consider results with some match potential if analysis['match_score'] >= 2: match_data = { 'query_number': i, 'position': result.get('position', 0), 'title': result['title'], 'link': result['link'], 'snippet': result['snippet'], **analysis } query_matches.append(match_data) print(f" üéØ MATCH #{result.get('position', '?')}: {result['title'][:50]}...") print(f" Score: {analysis['match_score']}/6 | Confidence: {analysis['confidence']}") print(f" URL: {result['link'][:70]}...") # Show matched criteria matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in analysis['criteria'].items() if v] print(f" ‚úÖ Matched: {', '.join(matched)}") if 'youtube.com' in result['link'] or 'youtu.be' in result['link']: print(f" üì∫ YOUTUBE VIDEO CONFIRMED") # Extract video ID if 'watch?v=' in result['link']: try: video_id = result['link'].split('watch?v=')[1].split('&')[0] print(f" üÜî Video ID: {video_id}") except: pass if analysis['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH CONFIDENCE - Likely target!") elif analysis['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚úÖ HIGH CONFIDENCE - Strong candidate") print() # Store query results results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'total_results': len(search_results), 'matches_found': len(query_matches), 'matches': query_matches, 'status': 'success' }) results['all_matches'].extend(query_matches) print(f"Query {i} complete: {len(query_matches)} matches found") else: print(f"‚ùå Search failed: {status}") results['query_results'].append({ 'query_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'status': status }) # Respectful delay if i < len(search_queries): delay = 3 print(f"Waiting {delay}s before next query...") time.sleep(delay) # Analyze final results print(f"\n=== FINAL RESULTS ANALYSIS ===") total_matches = len(results['all_matches']) print(f"Total potential matches found: {total_matches}") if total_matches > 0: # Sort by match score and confidence sorted_matches = sorted( results['all_matches'], key=lambda x: (x['match_score'], x['confidence'] == 'very_high', x['confidence'] == 'high'), reverse=True ) print(f"\nüèÜ TOP CANDIDATES FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO:\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:3], 1): print(f"{i}. SCORE: {match['match_score']}/6 | CONFIDENCE: {match['confidence'].upper().replace('_', ' ')}") print(f" Title: {match['title']}") print(f" URL: {match['link']}") if match['snippet']: print(f" Description: {match['snippet'][:150]}...") matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria'].items() if v] missing = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria'].items() if not v] print(f" ‚úÖ Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched)}") print(f" ‚ùå Missing: {', '.join(missing)}") if 'youtube.com' in match['link']: print(f" üì∫ CONFIRMED YOUTUBE VIDEO") if 'watch?v=' in match['link']: try: video_id = match['link'].split('watch?v=')[1].split('&')[0] print(f" üîó Direct link: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}") except: pass if match['match_score'] >= 5: print(f" üéØ VERY LIKELY TARGET VIDEO!") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: print(f" ‚≠ê STRONG CANDIDATE") print() # Calculate summary statistics youtube_matches = len([m for m in results['all_matches'] if 'youtube.com' in m['link'] or 'youtu.be' in m['link']]) high_confidence = len([m for m in results['all_matches'] if m['confidence'] in ['very_high', 'high']]) results['summary'] = { 'total_matches': total_matches, 'youtube_videos': youtube_matches, 'high_confidence_matches': high_confidence, 'top_match_score': sorted_matches[0]['match_score'] if sorted_matches else 0, 'search_success': True } print(f"üìä SEARCH STATISTICS:") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Total matches: {total_matches}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ YouTube videos: {youtube_matches}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ High confidence: {high_confidence}") print(f" ‚Ä¢ Top score: {results['summary']['top_match_score']}/6") else: results['summary'] = { 'total_matches': 0, 'search_success': False } print(f"‚ùå No potential matches found") # Save comprehensive results final_results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'corrected_scraping_results.json') with open(final_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) print(f"\nüìÅ Results saved to: {os.path.basename(final_results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(final_results_file):,} bytes") # Create final summary report if total_matches > 0: summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'ANDY_SERKIS_FINAL_RESULTS.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write("ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO - SEARCH RESULTS\n") f.write("=" * 55 + "\n\n") f.write(f"Search Date: {results['search_metadata']['execution_date']}\n") f.write(f"Method: {results['search_metadata']['method']}\n") f.write(f"Total Candidates: {total_matches}\n\n") f.write("üéØ TARGET CRITERIA:\n") f.write(" ‚úì Format: 360 VR\n") f.write(" ‚úì Date: March 2018\n") f.write(" ‚úì Content: Dinosaurs\n") f.write(" ‚úì Narrator: Andy Serkis\n\n") f.write("üèÜ TOP CANDIDATE VIDEOS:\n\n") for i, match in enumerate(sorted_matches[:3], 1): f.write(f"{i}. {match['title']}\n") f.write(f" URL: {match['link']}\n") f.write(f" Score: {match['match_score']}/6 | Confidence: {match['confidence'].replace('_', ' ').title()}\n") matched = [k.replace('_', ' ').title() for k, v in match['criteria'].items() if v] f.write(f" Criteria Met: {', '.join(matched)}\n") if match['match_score'] >= 5: f.write(f" ‚≠ê VERY HIGH PROBABILITY\n") elif match['match_score'] >= 4: f.write(f" ‚úÖ HIGH PROBABILITY\n") f.write("\n") f.write(f"VERIFICATION STEPS:\n") f.write(f"1. Confirm dinosaur content\n") print(f"üìÑ Summary report: {os.path.basename(summary_file)}") print(f"\n‚úÖ CORRECTED WEB SCRAPING COMPLETE") if total_matches > 0: print(f"üéâ SUCCESS: Found {total_matches} potential videos") print(f"üì∫ {results['summary']['youtube_videos']} YouTube videos identified") if results['summary']['high_confidence_matches'] > 0: print(f"‚≠ê {results['summary']['high_confidence_matches']} high-confidence candidates") print(f"\nüîç Next: Verify top candidates manually using the provided URLs") else: print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è No matches found - may need different search approach") print(f"\nüìÇ All results in workspace: {workspace_dir}")
