import os import json from datetime import datetime import subprocess from urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs print("=== DIRECT YOUTUBE VIDEO SEARCH: ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEO ===") print("Previous automated search approaches failed due to anti-bot measures") print("Implementing direct video search strategy using known patterns and manual verification\n") # Create workspace directory workspace_dir = "workspace" os.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True) print(f"Workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\n") # Based on the search objective, let's try known YouTube video patterns # and use yt-dlp to search and verify videos print("=== STEP 1: SEARCHING FOR ANDY SERKIS 360 VR DINOSAUR VIDEOS ===\n") # Strategy: Use yt-dlp's search capabilities to find videos # This bypasses web scraping issues and uses YouTube's API more directly search_terms = [ "Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur", "Andy Serkis virtual reality dinosaur", "Andy Serkis 360 degree dinosaur", "Andy Serkis dinosaur experience VR", "Andy Serkis prehistoric 360" ] all_found_videos = [] search_results = [] for i, search_term in enumerate(search_terms, 1): print(f"Search {i}/{len(search_terms)}: '{search_term}'") try: # Use yt-dlp to search YouTube search_cmd = [ 'yt-dlp', f'ytsearch10:{search_term}', # Search for top 10 results '--dump-json', '--no-playlist', '--quiet' ] print(f" Executing: {' '.join(search_cmd)}") # Run the search command result = subprocess.run(search_cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=60) if result.returncode == 0 and result.stdout.strip(): print(f" ‚úÖ Search successful") # Parse each line as a separate JSON object (yt-dlp outputs one JSON per line) video_data_lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\n') search_videos = [] for line in video_data_lines: if line.strip(): try: video_info = json.loads(line) # Extract key information title = video_info.get('title', 'Unknown Title') video_id = video_info.get('id', 'Unknown ID') url = video_info.get('webpage_url', f'https://youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}') uploader = video_info.get('uploader', 'Unknown Uploader') duration = video_info.get('duration', 0) upload_date = video_info.get('upload_date', 'Unknown Date') view_count = video_info.get('view_count', 0) description = video_info.get('description', '')[:500] # First 500 chars # Analyze relevance title_lower = title.lower() description_lower = description.lower() uploader_lower = uploader.lower() # Check for Andy Serkis has_andy_serkis = any(term in text for text in [title_lower, description_lower, uploader_lower] for term in ['andy serkis', 'serkis']) # Check for 360/VR content has_360_vr = any(term in text for text in [title_lower, description_lower] for term in ['360', 'vr', 'virtual reality', '360¬∞', 'immersive']) # Check for dinosaur content has_dinosaur = any(term in text for text in [title_lower, description_lower] for term in ['dinosaur', 'prehistoric', 'jurassic', 'cretaceous', 'fossil', 'extinct']) # Check for 2018 content has_2018 = '2018' in upload_date or '2018' in title_lower or '2018' in description_lower # Check for March 2018 specifically has_march_2018 = False if upload_date and len(upload_date) >= 6: try: year_month = upload_date[:6] # YYYYMM format has_march_2018 = year_month == '201803' except: pass # Calculate relevance score relevance_score = 0 if has_andy_serkis: relevance_score += 5 if has_360_vr: relevance_score += 4 if has_dinosaur: relevance_score += 4 if has_march_2018: relevance_score += 3 elif has_2018: relevance_score += 2 video_data = { 'title': title, 'video_id': video_id, 'url': url, 'uploader': uploader, 'duration_seconds': duration, 'duration_formatted': f"{duration//60}:{duration%60:02d}" if duration else "Unknown", 'upload_date': upload_date, 'view_count': view_count, 'description_preview': description, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'match_criteria': { 'has_andy_serkis': has_andy_serkis, 'has_360_vr': has_360_vr, 'has_dinosaur': has_dinosaur, 'has_2018': has_2018, 'has_march_2018': has_march_2018 }, 'search_term': search_term } search_videos.append(video_data) all_found_videos.append(video_data) if relevance_score >= 8: # Very high relevance print(f" üéØ EXCELLENT MATCH (Score: {relevance_score}): {title[:60]}...") print(f" Video ID: {video_id}") print(f" URL: {url}") print(f" Uploader: {uploader}") print(f" Upload Date: {upload_date}") print(f" Duration: {video_data['duration_formatted']}") elif relevance_score >= 5: print(f" ‚≠ê GOOD MATCH (Score: {relevance_score}): {title[:60]}...") print(f" Video ID: {video_id}") except json.JSONDecodeError as e: print(f" ‚ö†Ô∏è JSON parse error: {str(e)}") continue search_results.append({ 'search_term': search_term, 'videos_found': len(search_videos), 'status': 'success' }) print(f" üìä Found {len(search_videos)} videos for this search term\n") else: print(f" ‚ùå Search failed or no results") if result.stderr: print(f" Error: {result.stderr[:200]}...") search_results.append({ 'search_term': search_term, 'status': 'failed', 'error': result.stderr[:500] if result.stderr else 'No output' }) print() except subprocess.TimeoutExpired: print(f" ‚è∞ Search timed out after 60 seconds") search_results.append({ 'search_term': search_term, 'status': 'timeout' }) print() except Exception as e: print(f" ‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}") search_results.append({ 'search_term': search_term, 'status': 'error', 'error': str(e) }) print() print("=== SEARCH RESULTS ANALYSIS ===\n") # Remove duplicates based on video ID unique_videos = [] seen_video_ids = set() for video in all_found_videos: if video['video_id'] not in seen_video_ids: unique_videos.append(video) seen_video_ids.add(video['video_id']) print(f"Total videos found: {len(all_found_videos)}") print(f"Unique videos after deduplication: {len(unique_videos)}") # Sort by relevance score unique_videos.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) # Show top results print(f"\n=== TOP 10 MOST RELEVANT VIDEOS ===\n") top_candidates = [] for i, video in enumerate(unique_videos[:10], 1): print(f"{i}. {video['title']}") print(f" Video ID: {video['video_id']}") print(f" URL: {video['url']}") print(f" Uploader: {video['uploader']}") print(f" Duration: {video['duration_formatted']}") print(f" Upload Date: {video['upload_date']}") print(f" Views: {video['view_count']:,}" if video['view_count'] else " Views: Unknown") print(f" Relevance Score: {video['relevance_score']}") print(f" Match Criteria: {video['match_criteria']}") print(f" Description Preview: {video['description_preview'][:100]}...") print() if video['relevance_score'] >= 8: top_candidates.append(video) # Save comprehensive results results_data = { 'search_metadata': { 'search_date': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'search_method': 'yt-dlp YouTube search', 'objective': 'Find Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur video from March 2018', 'total_search_terms': len(search_terms), 'total_videos_found': len(all_found_videos), 'unique_videos': len(unique_videos) }, 'search_terms': search_terms, 'search_results': search_results, 'all_videos': unique_videos, 'top_candidates': top_candidates, 'analysis_summary': { 'highest_relevance_score': max([v['relevance_score'] for v in unique_videos]) if unique_videos else 0, 'videos_with_excellent_relevance': len([v for v in unique_videos if v['relevance_score'] >= 8]), 'videos_with_andy_serkis': len([v for v in unique_videos if v['match_criteria']['has_andy_serkis']]), 'videos_with_360_vr': len([v for v in unique_videos if v['match_criteria']['has_360_vr']]), 'videos_with_dinosaur': len([v for v in unique_videos if v['match_criteria']['has_dinosaur']]), 'videos_from_march_2018': len([v for v in unique_videos if v['match_criteria']['has_march_2018']]), 'videos_from_2018': len([v for v in unique_videos if v['match_criteria']['has_2018']]) } } # Save results results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'andy_serkis_video_search_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"üìÅ Comprehensive search results saved to: {os.path.basename(results_file)}") print(f"File size: {os.path.getsize(results_file):,} bytes") # Final analysis and recommendations print(f"\n=== FINAL SEARCH ANALYSIS ===\n") successful_searches = len([r for r in search_results if r['status'] == 'success']) print(f"Search Success Rate: {successful_searches}/{len(search_terms)} ({successful_searches/len(search_terms)*100:.1f}%)") print(f"Total Unique Videos Found: {len(unique_videos)}") print(f"Videos with Excellent Relevance (‚â•8): {results_data['analysis_summary']['videos_with_excellent_relevance']}") print(f"Videos mentioning Andy Serkis: {results_data['analysis_summary']['videos_with_andy_serkis']}") print(f"Videos with 360/VR content: {results_data['analysis_summary']['videos_with_360_vr']}") print(f"Videos with dinosaur content: {results_data['analysis_summary']['videos_with_dinosaur']}") print(f"Videos from March 2018: {results_data['analysis_summary']['videos_from_march_2018']}") print(f"Videos from 2018: {results_data['analysis_summary']['videos_from_2018']}") if top_candidates: print(f"\nüéØ EXCELLENT CANDIDATES FOUND ({len(top_candidates)} videos):") for i, candidate in enumerate(top_candidates, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {candidate['title']}") print(f" Video ID: {candidate['video_id']}") print(f" URL: {candidate['url']}") print(f" Relevance Score: {candidate['relevance_score']}") print(f" Upload Date: {candidate['upload_date']}") print(f" Match Criteria: {candidate['match_criteria']}") # Select the best candidate for analysis best_candidate = top_candidates[0] # Save best candidate for next step candidate_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'target_video_for_analysis.json') with open(candidate_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'objective': 'Analyze Andy Serkis 360 VR dinosaur video for dinosaur appearance timing', 'target_video': best_candidate, 'analysis_tasks': [ 'Download video content', 'Identify when dinosaurs first appear in the video', 'Document the specific number mentioned by narrator after dinosaur appearance', 'Extract relevant timestamps and context' ], 'next_step': 'Video download and content analysis' }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\nüìÅ Target video saved to: {os.path.basename(candidate_file)}") print(f"\n‚úÖ SEARCH PHASE SUCCESSFUL") print(f"Ready to proceed with video content analysis of: {best_candidate['title']}") print(f"Video URL: {best_candidate['url']}") elif unique_videos: print(f"\n‚ö†Ô∏è No excellent candidates found, but {len(unique_videos)} videos discovered") print(f"Top video by relevance score:") top_video = unique_videos[0] print(f" Title: {top_video['title']}") print(f" Score: {top_video['relevance_score']}") print(f" URL: {top_video['url']}") print(f"\nConsider analyzing this video or refining search criteria") else: print(f"\n‚ùå No videos found matching search criteria") print(f"Recommendations:") print(f" - The specific video may not exist or be publicly available") print(f" - Try different search terms or date ranges") print(f" - Check if the video was removed or made private") print(f"\n=== VIDEO SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ===") print(f"Search method: yt-dlp direct YouTube search") print(f"Results saved to workspace: {workspace_dir}")
